  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_83a07a39-7d77-48e5-9bbf-04d2ea347ffa'
      });
    }

      var APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL =  "https://appleid.cdn-apple.com/appleauth/static/jsapi/appleid/1/en_US/appleid.auth.js"

<span id="freeTextContainer14224281725176277848">Have you ever heard of the old Celtic legends of the Fae—beautiful, magical, and deadly creatures that have a love of messing with humans just for kicks and giggles?<br/><br/>Welcome to my world.<br/><br/>What started out as a strange assignment, led to one of the most gruesome murder mysteries of our times.   <span id="freeText14224281725176277848" style="display:none">Have you ever heard of the old Celtic legends of the Fae—beautiful, magical, and deadly creatures that have a love of messing with humans just for kicks and giggles?<br /><br />Welcome to my world.<br /><br />What started out as a strange assignment, led to one of the most gruesome murder mysteries of our times. My friends and I are set and determined to find out who is killing off Fae and Witches alike.<br /><br />Couple of problems in the way – I hate the Fae and the Prince of the Dark Fae is bound and determined that I work for him. He’s a rude, overbearing egotistical ass with a compulsive need to possess, dominate and control me. Oh—did I mention that he is absolutely sex-on-a-stick gorgeous and he makes me feel things that I never ever wanted to feel for a Fae... every time he touches me or looks at me with those dangerous golden eyes he seems to pull me further in under his spell, despite my better judgment.<br /><br />My friends and I can’t trust anyone and nothing is as it seems on the surface—not even me.</span>

<div id="review_678401214" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/678401214" />
    <a title="Erin" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/6949434-erin"><img alt="Erin" src="https://s.gr-assets.com/assets/nophoto/user/f_50x66-6a03a5c12233c941481992b82eea8d23.png" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/678401214?book_show_action=true">Jul 27, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Erin" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Erin" href="/user/show/6949434-erin">Erin</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="did not like it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">did not like it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer678401214" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer7973835464951661599">I cannot even begin to fathom how this book has gotten such a high rating. The main character is annoying and constantly makes terrible decisions that end with her being "owned" and then complains for a while, but apparently actually enjoys it deep down because not having free will and being forced into situations where a hot guy could rape you if he felt like it, but chooses not to (making him honorable apparently) is extremely hot and romantic. Also, it's apparently completely okay to trick a </span>
  <span id="freeText7973835464951661599" style="display:none">I cannot even begin to fathom how this book has gotten such a high rating. The main character is annoying and constantly makes terrible decisions that end with her being "owned" and then complains for a while, but apparently actually enjoys it deep down because not having free will and being forced into situations where a hot guy could rape you if he felt like it, but chooses not to (making him honorable apparently) is extremely hot and romantic. Also, it's apparently completely okay to trick a girl into having to have sex with you in order to prevent being raped be the next dude that comes by. This apparently is not rape because she "chooses" him rather than choosing to fight off countless others who would come after her and most likely rape her otherwise.<br />Then, if all these scenes where the line between rape and consent are incredibly blurred aren't bad enough, there's the way this guy is constantly seeking to control her, demands answers he really doesn't deserve, and lacks total empathy. I mean who the hell forces a girl that he's employing and has only just met to relive her parents murder so he can find out what happened to her even though it has nothing to do with the case he hired her for and then has the nerve to ask why he wasn't notified of her circumstances, like it was any of his business what she went through?<br />Moral of the story: 1. It's not rape if he's hot. 2. Abusive, controlling relationships are romantic, if he's hot.</span>
  <a data-text-id="7973835464951661599" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

  <span id="freeText4083747950807667584" style="display:none"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1391758822i/8450794.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><a href="http://www.amazon.com/Fighting-Destiny-Chronicles-Amelia-Hutchins-ebook/dp/B00D5M4PTM/ref=sr_sp-atf_title_1_1?s=books&amp;ie=UTF8&amp;qid=1391755189&amp;sr=1-1&amp;keywords=9780991190904" rel="nofollow noopener">Amazon</a><br><a href="http://www.barnesandnoble.com/w/fighting-destiny-amelia-hutchins/1116968040?ean=9780991190911" rel="nofollow noopener">Barnes and Noble</a><br><a href="http://www.smashwords.com/books/view/322315" rel="nofollow noopener">Smashwords</a><br><br><b>5 Scorching Hot Stars!</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1389980172i/8118771.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Fighting Destiny by Amy Hutchins is the first book in <i>The Fae Chronicles</i><br><br><b>What an absolutely fun and exciting introduction to a series</b><br><br>The first book packs a serious punch, we're introduced to Syn, as she and her coven take on a very difficult assignment; what starts out as a very challenging assignment turns into something completely different and unexpected.<br><br>When Syn and the Dark Prince meet, their relationship is complex... They might not like each other but they have this inexplicable attraction, two sworn enemies who can't keep their hands off each other. Now when I say they couldn't keep their hands off each other I'm was serious, when it comes to these two together, they don't need much to set them off.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1390176512i/8158073._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Syn is a witch, the only thing she cares about is avenging her parents death and protecting her coven. She hates everything about the Fae especially the Prince of the Dark Fae, Ryder.<br><br>When they meet, she's horrified at the attraction she feels for him, and avoids him at all costs. Too bad he won't let her.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1390176512i/8158074._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Ryder is the prince of the dark fae, he's ruthless and unpredictable. When he sees Syn, he might not like her but that won't stop him from having her. Her resistance makes the chase even better. His past is a mystery and as the story progresses we get clues and insight giving us a tiny picture of why he does the things he does...<br><br>Syn and Ryder suffered from a serious case of "I hate you so much that I wanna f#ck you" syndrome. Their anger would always lead to them mauling each other against some surface, and I absolutely loved it!<br><br>I'm not a huge fan of Syn (she was little bit too blonde and beautiful) but her personality complimented Ryder's perfectly. Ryder was the perfect alpha male in my opinion, he was over bearing, rude and 100% hot!<br><br>If you're looking for a fun and sexy PNR, this is it! The first book in the series was unputdownable!<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1390042072ra/8133085.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></span>

<span id="freeTextContainer18145448275637009406">Maybe it's the cover but I honestly wasn't expecting this to be very good but it was free so I downloaded it on my kindle to read anyways. The story line kept me engaged the whole time though and the pacing was really good. It's excellent for what it is which is a fantasy/erotica novel and the only thing I found wanting was the writing but again even though it was slightly juvenile it works because it's not really a literature book it works fine in its genre. Definitely want to read the next one</span>
  <span id="freeText18145448275637009406" style="display:none">Maybe it's the cover but I honestly wasn't expecting this to be very good but it was free so I downloaded it on my kindle to read anyways. The story line kept me engaged the whole time though and the pacing was really good. It's excellent for what it is which is a fantasy/erotica novel and the only thing I found wanting was the writing but again even though it was slightly juvenile it works because it's not really a literature book it works fine in its genre. Definitely want to read the next one in the series.<br /><br /></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer858685878" class="readable"

<span id="freeTextContainer7788029712238359417"><b>5 Brilliant Scorching Stars</b><br/><br/><i>Kickass Heroine ✓<br/>Badass Hero ✓<br/>Non-stop Action ✓<br/>Otherwordly hot, panties-dropping, sheets-on-fire Sex ✓<br/>Actual plot, sex aside ✓</i><br/><br/><pre>THIS BOOK....</pre><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380411635ra/808894.gif' width='400' height='220' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>A new paranormal romance series that thank God, proved to be so much more!<br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380401448ra/779251.gif' width='400' height='210' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380423531ra/843809.gif' width='400' height='200' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>We are living in a new reality where supernatural creatures made their existence known to mankind. Now it's a different world where vampires bump freely into the night, the Guild of Witches keep people safe and Fae rule them all with an iron hand. Dangerous, l</span>
  <span id="freeText7788029712238359417" style="display:none"><b>5 Brilliant Scorching Stars</b><br><br><i>Kickass Heroine ✓<br>Badass Hero ✓<br>Non-stop Action ✓<br>Otherwordly hot, panties-dropping, sheets-on-fire Sex ✓<br>Actual plot, sex aside ✓</i><br><br><pre>THIS BOOK....</pre><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380411635ra/808894.gif" width="400" height="220" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>A new paranormal romance series that thank God, proved to be so much more!<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380401448ra/779251.gif" width="400" height="210" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380423531ra/843809.gif" width="400" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>We are living in a new reality where supernatural creatures made their existence known to mankind. Now it's a different world where vampires bump freely into the night, the Guild of Witches keep people safe and Fae rule them all with an iron hand. Dangerous, lethal and seductive they are a dream and a nightmare at the same time and they know how to keep their secrets...<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1393323572i/8694567.jpg" width="300" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>In this world, <b>Synthia</b> is a member of the Guild, an orphan that everyone she gets close to, dies. A badass witch with a grudge against all Fae and determined to see them fall.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380415993ra/821439.gif" width="400" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>Ryder</b> the Dark Prince of the Fae has his own agenda and he is lethal as he is seductive. A man of many secrets, primal and dangerous.<br><br><b>
  <i>She should run but I'd catch her. I always catch my prey. I take because I can, because no one else can stop me. I am what she fears. I can smell it coming off her in succulent waves and it drives my inner beast insane</i>
</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1393323572ra/8694568.gif" width="400" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1393051966ra/8654701.gif" width="400" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Together, they are investigating a string of murders that will rock their worlds, will unbury secrets and unravel mysteries and ultimately will bring them together and threaten to disturb the precarious balance between their realms. An attraction that they can't deny.<br><br><b>
  <i>She may hate me when it is over - I'll face that when we get there. Until then, I plan to make her mine in body and soul.</i>
</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380433838ra/873354.gif" width="400" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Getting each other out of their systems leads surprisingly to more. But they aren't ready yet to just give in and reveal their truths.<br><br><b>
  <i>-I'll be strong for you Syn... If you need it. You don't always have to be the strong one. I'll be your glue if you want to crumble. I'll hold you together.<br>-And what if you're what's making me crumble, Ryder?</i>
</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380436029ra/881098.gif" width="400" height="280" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Excellent worldbuilding, multi-layered, complex characters, intrigue, mystery, sex, heartbreak this book has it all. And I mean ALL!!! Addictive, emotional and.......... f*cking PERFECT! And then there are the last chapters and revelations and pain and that ending!!<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380430107ra/862220.gif" width="400" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>It is not every day that you read a paranormal romance and you feel that you can relate to the characters and the situations. It helps that this is a series so we get a lot of insight in the heroes and we watch them struggle and grow. Nothing is really resolved so you are left craving for more and trying to put off the fire in your bedroom. <br><br>Can't wait for more and what are you doing and you haven't read these books???<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1393323572ra/8694569.gif" width="400" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer675123939" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer14007923223358994459"><b>First re-read: 20.10.14</b><br/><b>Second re-read: 23.04.15</b><br/><b>Third re-read: 13.11.2016</b><br/>Ummm....I think I need to let go of Ryder, or I'll never, ever, get a man. Seriously. He holds my heart so fucking close that I ... I don't know what to do. Man, I love Ryder to fucking much. Cyn's great, of course, but Ryder...damn, he's my fucking fantasy. <br/><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“Never challenge me, I promise that you will lose. Every. Fucking. Time.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1479009043i/21138759.png' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><b><u>Quick basic facts</u>:</b><br/><b>Genre</b>: - (Adult) Paranormal Romance<br/><b>Series</b>: - Series, Book One <br/><b>Love</b></span>
  <span id="freeText14007923223358994459" style="display:none"><b>First re-read: 20.10.14</b><br><b>Second re-read: 23.04.15</b><br><b>Third re-read: 13.11.2016</b><br>Ummm....I think I need to let go of Ryder, or I'll never, ever, get a man. Seriously. He holds my heart so fucking close that I ... I don't know what to do. Man, I love Ryder to fucking much. Cyn's great, of course, but Ryder...damn, he's my fucking fantasy. <br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“Never challenge me, I promise that you will lose. Every. Fucking. Time.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1479009043i/21138759.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><b><u>Quick basic facts</u>:</b><br><b>Genre</b>: - (Adult) Paranormal Romance<br><b>Series</b>: - Series, Book One <br><b>Love triangle?</b> - <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[No, not really. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><b>Cheating?</b> - <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[No. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><b>HEA?</b> - <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[No, cliffy. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><b>Favorite character?</b> - Ryder Dé Danann<br><b>Would I read more by this author/or of series?</b> - Do I even have to answer that? If so, yes!<br><b>Would I recommend this book/series?</b> - Fuck yes.<br><b>Will I read this again in the future?</b> - It's Ryder, what do you think?<br><b>Rating</b> - 4.5-5 *fucking fairy* stars.<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1445268775i/16623124.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><b>First read review:</b><br><u>Fighting Destiny by Amelia Hutchins</u><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>Syn is scared. She should be fucking terrified. I want her and nothing will stop me now. Not even her newly risen love, if he gets in the way he will really go to his grave, I own him now. Another fucking pawn, on my growing board. His supposed death broke her, I intend to pick up those pieces and use them to get inside her beautiful fucked up mind.</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>When Syn, a kick-ass-heroine witch, started working out on a strange assignment, lead to one of the most gruesome murder mysteries of their times. Her friends and the Dark Fae are set and determined to find out who is killing off Fae and Witches alike... While trying to found out who the murderers are, Ryder is pulling Syn further in under his spell, despite her better judgment. Syn and her friends can’t trust anyone and nothing is as it seems on the surface – not even herself.<br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>The Dark Prince stood before me, his hair so black that it almost appeared blue in the lights. Golden eyes stared at me, no emotion in their endless depths, at all. He was the most beautiful thing I had ever seen. </i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>Ryder usually get's what he wants, but he never expected that he would want a snappy, irritated witch. He didn't expect to get Syn in his plans. He wants Syn like he never wanted anyone before and he hates it. He loves control, he needs it, and so does Syn. Syn hates fairies because of her brutal past. So when she's pressed in to a corner, she has no choice but to agree to work for the Prince of the Dark Fae. She's forced to sign a contract, which she of course is stupid enough not to read before she does... <br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“I’m not a piece of fucking property, I cannot be owned!”<br>“Quite the opposite, you are mine. As of right now, you belong to me Pet.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>Syn is a witch who takes shit from no one. She's snappy, fast and powerful. She's what you could call a kick-ass-heroine. Syn is strong and has a really good heart, and at the same time she doesn't make herself weak because she has a kind heart. She's been trough hell and back again, and she still is standing, which she deserves a hell of a lot credit for! Syn's the kind of person who really learns from her mistakes and she makes the pain and the anger she feels to become stronger, to fight her fears. Syn's got a biiiiig mouth that she uses a lot, and has her perfect comebacks. She's actually funny as hell.<br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>It won’t be enough to sate the hunger I feel inside for her, but it will be enough to brand her skin and mark her as my own. Then no one can question who she belongs to. She’s mine. And I will have her in every fucking way possible, until she becomes a problem. I’ll cross that bridge when I get to it. Until then, I plan to take her until she only knows one name—mine. </i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>Ryder, got damn Ryder, the Prince of the Dark Fae.. Powerful, dangerous, sexy as fuck. He's stubborn and dominate, and hot as hell. He's rich, overbearing egotistical ass of a bastard who gets exactly what he wants. If he plays a game, well... he always wins.. Ryder's the guy your parents would NEVER agree to dating their daughter. But damn, he's irresistible! He's got one hell of a dark side, and a healthy person would stay the hell out of his way. Though he's incredible dangerous, you still get to see soft sides of him, where Ryder's gentle and caring, and you simply can't help but to fall for him. He's protective, and possessive as fuck. Ryder's smart, and knows how to play, and he's an really old fae. Ryder's really mysterious, and doesn't really share his personal life.<br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"..Love is more than just feeling something Syn, it’s the connection of two souls that intertwine and cannot be without the other. It’s not just saying you love someone, its showing them with every fucking breath you take, every look. It just is, simple as that. That kind of love doesn’t die. It withers the soul without the other to keep it alive. Eventually, it turns you bitter and cynical.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>Ryder and Syn's story was impressive. I really loved how their relationship developed from hate to 'kinda friendship' to perhaps more...<br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“Be as that as it may, I told the guard you were mine. You stole my car.”<br>“Borrowed it I did, return it I will.”<br>Oh bloody fucking hell.<br>“Okay Yoda, can I have the woman whose body you stole back?”<br>“My body it is, yours I am not. Dead I speak until drained I am,” I smiled unable to help myself. </i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>I love this book! It's was incredible and well written. Amelia Hutchins really know's how to capture a reader! I was obsessed after the first couple of pages... The book didn't really get boring at all, and something happened all the time. You got the information you needed, and it's never got too much.. Sometimes in other books you get a lot of unnecessary info and it's sometimes makes the book boring and hard to read. But Fighting Destiny gave you exactly what you needed and nothing more. I love how Amelia wrote the characters! I also love that she even wrote in Ryder's POV, which was great, cause then you get the see what's on his dark mind.. In my opinion, I felt like Ryder got softer towards Syn on each POV from him. Which made me love him even more.. Damn him! <br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“I’ll be strong for you Syn, if you need it. You don’t always have to be the strong one, I’ll be your glue if you want to crumble, I’ll hold you together,” he said lifting his eyes and meeting mine.<br>“And what if you’re what’s making me crumble Ryder, what then?”<br>His lips lifted into his sexy smirk. “Then I’ll put you back together. I will never tear you down Syn. I will always protect you from anything and everything that would. I’ve yet to find anything in this world or any other who can take me on—keep that in mind,” he said lifting his eyes to meet mine before he started to turn away.<br>I was startled by his words and what he had said earlier when we were dancing. He didn’t like me, did he? “That’s what I’m afraid of.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>I felt connected with Syn and it was awesome. Like, as soon as I started to read everything disappeared except the book. This book had it all! A dominated alpha male, a kick-ass-heroine, sexy sweet sex, friendship and loyalty, tears and laughter. I can't wait to read the next book. Can't wait for the story about Syn and Ryder to continue! <br><br><b>Rate: 4.5-5 stars.</b></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>
  <a data-text-id="14007923223358994459" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<span id="freeTextContainer17822994321177638468">This started off SO strong and I was enthralled. <br/><br/>But then you throw in some minor plot holes, some major characterization inconsistencies, some personality vs. action issues, and some semi-flawed world-building and we are left with a bit of a convoluted...mess, honestly.<br/><br/>Regardless, I really did enjoy it and I am intrigued by the questions we are left with at the end of book one. I want to know...WHO exactly is Ryder, WHY exactly is Syn so important, and WHAT exactly is their destiny?<br/><br/>*Side Note: </span>
  <span id="freeText17822994321177638468" style="display:none">This started off SO strong and I was enthralled. <br><br>But then you throw in some minor plot holes, some major characterization inconsistencies, some personality vs. action issues, and some semi-flawed world-building and we are left with a bit of a convoluted...mess, honestly.<br><br>Regardless, I really did enjoy it and I am intrigued by the questions we are left with at the end of book one. I want to know...WHO exactly is Ryder, WHY exactly is Syn so important, and WHAT exactly is their destiny?<br><br>*Side Note: This has been sitting on my kindle for over a year now. I got it for FREE and and it is the first book in my quest to kill my tbr of free/sale books that I have currently overloading my kindle. I'm proud of myself for getting started on it and doubly glad I enjoyed the book.<br><br><b>And PS. Supposedly Ryder is hung like a horse.         rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>


          <div><span class="uitext greyText">Recommends it for: </span>

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer872766086" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer11113289188594795289"><b>WOW!! I am in Love with Ryder!! <br/>He gets 4.5 "Dirtiest Talker EVER" stars<br/><br/><i>Ryder was not the kind of man you walked away from. You crawled on hands and knees, trying to remember who you had been before his touch corrupted you.</i><br/><br/><br/>Ryder, The Fae Dark Prince<br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1434647774i/15248263.png' width='400' height='400' alt='Ryder' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/></b><br/><br/><br/>So Ladies, I have read a LOT of mixed reviews on this book. Apparently it's a love it or hate it kinda series. If you like your men with Stalkerific tendencies, that stake their claim and tell you that you are their property, and show no emotion while</span>
  <span id="freeText11113289188594795289" style="display:none"><b>WOW!! I am in Love with Ryder!! <br>He gets 4.5 "Dirtiest Talker EVER" stars<br><br><i>Ryder was not the kind of man you walked away from. You crawled on hands and knees, trying to remember who you had been before his touch corrupted you.</i><br><br><br>Ryder, The Fae Dark Prince<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1434647774i/15248263.png" width="400" height="400" alt="Ryder" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></b><br><br><br>So Ladies, I have read a LOT of mixed reviews on this book. Apparently it's a love it or hate it kinda series. If you like your men with Stalkerific tendencies, that stake their claim and tell you that you are their property, and show no emotion while doing it (just an all consuming lust), then Ryder is the man for you. <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[But fierce emotions do come by book 2 of the series ;o))  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br><br><br><b>
  <i>"You are mine, Synthia. If any other feeds from you he will die. Do you understand what I am telling you?"<br>"I belong to no one,"<br>"Wrong. I'm claiming you, Syn. Right now, right here, you are mine."</i>
</b><br><br><br>I just Love that Caveman!! "You are mine and don't dare look at another man or I will kill him!!" Yes, that turns me on. I enjoy it even more when the heroine is a strong woman, that fights against the lust, attraction haze, and denies this claim. <br><br><br><br> <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1437331580i/15572522._SY540_.jpg" width="400" height="574" alt="Syn" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br><br>And that is exactly what Syn does through out this book. She lusts for Ryder, but refuses to admit it. This makes for a Nuclear explosion when these two finally do come together!!<br><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1392564550ra/8578453.gif" width="400" height="225" alt="passion" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br><br><b>
  <i>The scent of her need makes me want to pull back the delicate petals of her flower and devour it, consume it, fuck it.</i>
</b><br><br><br><br><br>Oh and did I mention that Ryder is a dirty talker. He says things to Synthia that makes me blush and wish I were her. <br><br><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1437963851i/15651233.jpg" width="400" height="333" alt="lust" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br>Yes...these two bicker A LOT. But he is a 1000 year old Fae Dark Prince that is use to getting his way, and she is a stubborn headed Witch that hates ALL things Fae!!<br><br><br><br>Amidst all of this sexual tension, their is an overall plot that will suck you in. There is a serial killer that in not only killing immortal Fae, but also killing witches. I Totally enjoyed this book and will give it a solid 4.5 star because I have a feeling that the series will get better once Ryder admits that his obsession with Syn goes beyond lust, and involves his heart. I believe he loves her and is in denial. <br><br><br>Gosh, I am devouring this series and highly recommend to my friends that love the Caveman mentality. Which means, he is stubborn, in charge. and he claims his female weather she likes it or not. There is No Non-con though. He makes her beg for it eventually. Which is freakin HAWT!!! And Sexes her so well that they both beg for more!! </a><br/><br/><br/><b>Spoilers</b><br/><br/>Fighting Destiny is the First book in The Fae Chronicles Series. Witches and Fae are being killed left and right. It's Synthia's job as a witch in the Guild, to enforcing laws that protect humankind from the rest of the Otherworld creatures. Syn is the best at what she does, but she is a rebel with a dark past. Syn doesn't play well with others, and she hates and distrust the Fae. So she couldn't believe it when she was hired to work for the Dark P</span>
  <span id="freeText315125832395745780" style="display:none"><b> 4 The asses you hate to love Stars.</b><br><br><a href="http://s327.photobucket.com/user/jessica_hatfield1/media/9735314_zpsrxz5qep8.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1422497606ra/13506350.gif" alt=" photo 9735314_zpsrxz5qep8.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br><b>Spoilers</b><br><br>Fighting Destiny is the First book in The Fae Chronicles Series. Witches and Fae are being killed left and right. It's Synthia's job as a witch in the Guild, to enforcing laws that protect humankind from the rest of the Otherworld creatures. Syn is the best at what she does, but she is a rebel with a dark past. Syn doesn't play well with others, and she hates and distrust the Fae. So she couldn't believe it when she was hired to work for the Dark Prince of the Fae, Ryder. She doesn't trust Ryder, he is a rude ass jerk, use to getting what he wants, when he wants it, but she can't help the lust that burns in her for him. Ryder is powerful and he always gets what he wants. He doesn't ask, he takes. So when he wants the sassy witch that challenges everything he says and fighting him at every turn , no one will stop him from having her, not even her!<br><br>So this is the second time I have read this book. The first time I had a lot of mixed feelings about it. I liked it the first time, But I liked it more the second time around! There was parts of this book I really liked, but there where some parts of this book that I really didn't like.<br><br>Ryder:<br><br><a href="http://s327.photobucket.com/user/jessica_hatfield1/media/Ryderr1_zps7ogchi0c.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1422497606i/13506351._SX540_.jpg" alt=" photo Ryderr1_zps7ogchi0c.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br>Ryder confused the hell out of me one minute I liked him and the next I wanted to choke him. I think Ryder is kinda a dick. Sometimes he was this asshat that did things that I had a hard time seeing how Syn didn't just punch him in the throat. I had a hard time seeing how Syn could fall for him or trust him with the shit he pulled, then at other times he would do something sweet like have her dance on his feet. <br><br><a href="http://s327.photobucket.com/user/jessica_hatfield1/media/syn%20and%20ryder1_zpssbryx3r7.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1422497606i/13506352.jpg" alt=" photo syn and ryder1_zpssbryx3r7.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>It confused me and made me unsure of how I felt about Ryder. Also I have always said there is a difference between a sexy dominant alpha male and a crazy controlling borderline abusive male and I feel like the line was blurred in this book with Ryder. He was just too mean and controlling at times!<br><br><b>"Keep lipping off, and I'll find a use for that tongue." "Keep dreaming, man-whore."<br><br><br>"Never challenge me. I promise that you will lose. Every. Fucking. Time."<br><br><br><br>She's Challenging me. Even now, her eyes narrow on me, watching me as I watch her back hungrily. Challenge fucking accepted. ~ Ryder<br><br><br><br><br>"Then I'll put you back together. I will never tear you down, Syn. I will always protect you from anything and everything that would. I've yet to find anything in this world, or any other, who can take me on- keep that in mind,"</b><br><br>Synthia:<br><br><a href="http://s327.photobucket.com/user/jessica_hatfield1/media/syn1_zpspajaeobb.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1422497606i/13506353._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo syn1_zpspajaeobb.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br> <br><br>Synthia I liked a lot. I felt sorry for the things she lived through. She was very loyal to her friends who I didn't feel were very good friends to her at times. She was very sassy, and she has mad skills as a witch. At times she confused me too. She was kickass one minute and then she would let Ryder walk on her the next. <br><br><b>"I'm not a piece of fucking property! I cannot be owned!" <br><br><br>"I'm not like Claire, Ryder. I won't be used because you want sex. That's what it would be-right?"<br><br><br><br>"Fuck destiny. I decide my own destiny, Ryder. Not some fucking preordained bullshit,"</b><br><br><br><a href="http://s327.photobucket.com/user/jessica_hatfield1/media/syn%20and%20ryder1_zpsjo0myjhr.png.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1422497606i/13506354.png" alt=" photo syn and ryder1_zpsjo0myjhr.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Syn and Ryder's relationship while very hott with sexual tension and some very sexy dirty talk,<br><br><b>"You're too tight. I want to put my cock in you so fucking bad, Syn. I want to drive it in until you scream my name. Do you want it, Witch? Do you want this Fae cock fucking your tight pussy until it comes for me?"<br><br><br><br><br>"Fuck me, Ryder-hard. I'm asking you to just give it to me, everything. Stop holding it back."</b><br><br>lacked something for me. They had a Lust/ hate relationship for almost the whole book. I think that it was that I felt Ryder should have tried building her trust and showed her that she could trust fae, that they were not all alike and that not all would steal your will and rape and feed from you until you are a FIZ (Fae-induced zombie), but instead he was very selfish and broke her trust repeatedly. She even tried to give him a chance to earn her trust and to let him in, like their date. What does he do, He takes her to a hunt!!!<br><br><a href="http://s327.photobucket.com/user/jessica_hatfield1/media/punch%20face_zps2smkjywl.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1422497606ra/13506355.gif" alt=" photo punch face_zps2smkjywl.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br>The hunt where her choices where to sleep with him or he would let the next hunter have her and the next hunter wouldn't take no for an answer, so the hunter would rape her! Then if she chooses her ex boyfriend, Adrian at the hunt he would kill Adrian. So Syn basically had no choice!!! I am just not ok with that even if he does say:<br><br><b>"You want to be chased. You need the choice taken away from you. You fight your own desires, because you think you cannot handle it Syn. You punish yourself for something that happened long ago, something you couldn't have changed, because destiny decided it before you were even born. I'm just giving us both what we want."</b><br><br><br>I mean really? And she was ok with that and wanted to sleep with him pfff! Then after he and syn have sex for hours, he gets pulled from their bed to hear news that his people were attacked by witches. He believes they are from Syn's guild. So what does he do he chokes her, doesn't wait to find out what happens just decides Syn slept with him to set up the attack on his people. What a asshat again! I also didn't care for the FIZ mind control thing. I felt really sorry for Syn. She had a bad life and I felt trapped for her by Ryder and all the crap he pulls. Towards the end I think Ryder was confused by his own feelings for Syn and you do get to see him soften a little. I started to like the new sides that Ryder was showing. The ending OMG the ending was crazy making me Freak the freak out!<br> <br><a href="http://s327.photobucket.com/user/jessica_hatfield1/media/3205981_zpspiyid5na.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1422497606ra/13506356.gif" alt=" photo 3205981_zpspiyid5na.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>The story plot is great, the world was different in a good way, and it was written well and had lots of drama and plot twist. I can see that the book has the potential to become a great series depending on how the next book goes so I am on to the next book!<br><br><br><a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://jessicasoverthetopbookobsession.blogspot.com/">http://jessicasoverthetopbookobsessio...</a></span>

<span id="freeTextContainer2217998005531479731"><blockquote>
  <b>"It's not just saying you love someone—it’s showing them with every fucking breath you take, every look. It just is, simple as that."</b>
</blockquote><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1506185954i/23994692._SX540_.jpg' width='' height='' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><b>Fighting Destiny</b> is the first book in The Fae Chronicles Series. A seductive blend of passion, action, and romance set in a picturesque fantastical world makes <b>Fighting Destiny</b> an explosive start to this paranormal series.<br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1466701540i/19510149._SX540_.gif' width='' height='' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/> <blockquote>
  <b>"That kind of love doesn't die. It withers the soul without the other to keep it alive. Eventually, it turns you bitter and cynical.” </b>
</blockquote> I</span>
  <span id="freeText2217998005531479731" style="display:none"><blockquote>
  <b>"It's not just saying you love someone—it’s showing them with every fucking breath you take, every look. It just is, simple as that."</b>
</blockquote><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1506185954i/23994692._SX540_.jpg" width="" height="" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>Fighting Destiny</b> is the first book in The Fae Chronicles Series. A seductive blend of passion, action, and romance set in a picturesque fantastical world makes <b>Fighting Destiny</b> an explosive start to this paranormal series.<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1466701540i/19510149._SX540_.gif" width="" height="" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <blockquote>
  <b>"That kind of love doesn't die. It withers the soul without the other to keep it alive. Eventually, it turns you bitter and cynical.” </b>
</blockquote> In a world where witches and faes exist, the balance between life and death is in a constant battle. Synthia, a witch in the guild, is given an extraordinary assignment in which she is teamed up with one of her enemies Ryder (who happens to be the Dark Prince of the Fae). As Ryder and Synthia begin to bond, everything that Syn has ever been led to believe is put into question. As doubts continue to overtake her, Ryder is there to seduce her and give her affection and security like she has never felt before. But as tensions continue to rise between the witches and the fae, Syn and Ryder have much to overcome in order to find their way together. <blockquote>
  <b>“I can feel the draw, her body calling to mine as animals do in heat. I'd fuck her like an animal; raw, hot, and fucking hard.”</b>
</blockquote> <b>Fighting Destiny</b> is an absolute must for PRN fans! The sexual tension between Ryder and Syn is simply off the charts. The intricate world is full of intrigue and unique spiritual forces coming in from all directions. I am not going to lie there is ALOT going on in this world. The plot is complex and the characters have intense relationships. When you add in the magic, you will not be able to take your eyes away. There were certain moments during the read that I had an unbelievable desire to smack both Syn and Ryder but by the end, I was surprisingly entranced by this magical world and Ryder and Syn certainly had me coming back for more. Syn is definitely the standout character in this read for me. Her spunky "take no prisoners attitude" made her one of the strongest heroines I have ever met and Ryder is certainly her perfect match.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1466701540i/19510149._SX540_.gif" width="" height="" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Overall, I highly recommend <b>Fighting Destiny</b> to any and all PRN fans. Just be forewarned, this one ends in a major cliffy. Before starting this series, I highly recommend you download every single book in the series because once you start this journey, you will not want to stop. You will want your Kindle stocked and ready to go! <br><br><b>***The Fae Chronicles***<br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/17927559.Fighting_Destiny__The_Fae_Chronicles___1_" <span id="freeTextContainer388021795382451011">Fighting Destiny by Amelia Hutchins. <br/> <br/>My review of this book is me making comments while I'm reading the book. A lot of them are spoiler-ish so I'll spoiler-protect them. Stupid quips: Prince "Who do you work for?" She quipped sarcastically, "Your mother, she wants you to clean your bedroom." All this while she's chained to a wall waiting to die. Okay, my 7 year old neighbor could come up with more sarcasm than that. I don't know how the author's beta readers didn't mention how lame that phrase </span>
  <span id="freeText388021795382451011" style="display:none">Fighting Destiny by Amelia Hutchins. <br /> <br />My review of this book is me making comments while I'm reading the book. A lot of them are spoiler-ish so I'll spoiler-protect them. Stupid quips: Prince "Who do you work for?" She quipped sarcastically, "Your mother, she wants you to clean your bedroom." All this while she's chained to a wall waiting to die. Okay, my 7 year old neighbor could come up with more sarcasm than that. I don't know how the author's beta readers didn't mention how lame that phrase is. <br /><br /><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[I officially hate Ryder, he's the biggest, meanest Dick I think I've ever read. I think I would have killed myself by page 68. <br /><br />And her friends are useless and do not care for her at all. Her roommate knew about the "interview" and didn't tell her and even when Ryder pulls all kinds of horrible mind games and she gets angry about them not letting her know stuff so she wouldn't have killed someone, etc., Synthia feels bad for getting angry at them. Synthia, they're not true friends! <br /><br />Why is this book rated so high? I think it's doomed the book because I'm expecting perfection and I'm not finding it. <br /><br />Okay another peeve, Synthia keeps saying that she'll never do something he wants and then does it. Why doesn't she stop with these empty threats. Waste of breath and waste of reading time! <br /><br />Now his friend is calling him a "Damn fine man" making her second guess herself about him. Um, he had Synthia crawl to him in the dirt and beg him to let her orgasm even while she fought not to. That's rape buddy. <br /><br />Fancy Face, stupidest nickname ever! <br /><br />On one page, Ryder is imagining killing Syn and then in the next he's telling her how he will protect her because he protects what is his. Psycho! <br /><br />Now Ryder's invited her to a party which is really the Wild Hunt and if she doesn't have sex with him tonight, she has to have sex with the next hunter. And if she gets help during the hunt by an ex-boyfriend, Ryder will kill him. How in the hell is this a damn fine man?! <br /><br />Ryder tells Syn, she only reacts when something is taken from her so he's going to make her friend a Fae sex zombie. He's not a damn fine anything no matter what happens next.  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><br />Finally about 4/5 through the book it started to get good and then ended in a cliffhanger. I wish I could go back in time and not read this book but it was a group's monthly read. I'm not planning on reading this series. *1/2</span>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer738989803" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer7889642300992894926"><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1381487419i/4935345._SY540_.jpg' width='400' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><b> 4.5 sexy, kinky and fairy stars! </b><br/><br/>Fighting Destiny, totally wasn't what I expected it to be and this misunderstanding made me quickly fell in love with deliciously dark plot and kinky, alpha male Fae. Yep, you got that right, Ryder is dominant, sexy, perverted beast, that is a <i>Fae </i>. And not that kind of with wings and pink glitter. He's the Dark Prince, that likes to <i> own pretty little things </i> and feeds of sex. Weird, huh? I always pictured Fae as little fairies with odd ears and wearing thights</span>
  <span id="freeText7889642300992894926" style="display:none"><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1381487419i/4935345._SY540_.jpg" width="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b> 4.5 sexy, kinky and fairy stars! </b><br><br>Fighting Destiny, totally wasn't what I expected it to be and this misunderstanding made me quickly fell in love with deliciously dark plot and kinky, alpha male Fae. Yep, you got that right, Ryder is dominant, sexy, perverted beast, that is a <i>Fae </i>. And not that kind of with wings and pink glitter. He's the Dark Prince, that likes to <i> own pretty little things </i> and feeds of sex. Weird, huh? I always pictured Fae as little fairies with odd ears and wearing thights. But it's not the case in Amelia Hutchin's book. Here Fae are incredibly sexual and kinky creatures, that can make you orgasm multiply times and change you into sex slave that dies from being fucked. <br><br><b>
  <i>
    <u>
       "It was why they were considered the most deadly of the Otherworld.They could make you like it as they fucked you to death.." <br>
    </u>
  </i>
</b> <br><br>Syn is a kick ass girl. Probably one of the funniest, the most insane heroines I've read about in ages. She is everything I admire in strong women. The power war between her and Ryder was the most entertaining and the sexiest thing I've read about.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1381487419i/4935346._SX540_.jpg" width="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br> I felt glued to the pages, because of their constant banter, snarky comments and teasing. Syn's sassiness was great assest and it made this book extremely pleasurable read. But when she was mixed with the kind she hated the most and the sexiest yet annoying Fae that wanted to own her like a pet? It went from pleasurable to EXPLOSIVE. <br><br><b>
  <i>
    <u>
       “You ordered me here,” I said finally breaking the silence.<br>“I did,” Ryder said with his lopsided grin that looked more dangerous than friendly.<br>“I’m here,” I mumbled.<br>“You are.”<br>"..."<br>“Okay, we gonna measure dicks all day Ryder, or are we gonna sign a contract?” I snapped.<br>“You don’t have a dick Syn, I would have noticed,” Ryder’s smile lifted roguishly.” 
    </u>
  </i>
</b><br><br>Please, don't get me started on the sex parts because they were so, so hot, I melted... Ryder’s need to dominate, and Syn’s need to not feel owned, made the sex looks scorching, fight of dominance. I devoured every sexy snippet and drooled over Ryder magical ‘parts’. And that dirty mouth of his… God! I’m blushing while thinking about his words.<br><br><b>
  <i>
    <u>
      “I don’t make excuses for what I am, or what I do. I play hard. I love hard and I fuck even harder Syn, I am what I am. So if you play games with me, keep in mind I will be more than happy to play them with you—and I always win” 
    </u>
  </i>
</b><br><br>Ryder had also the other - swoonworthy side. Behind the bastard’s facade is hidden loveable man. I wish I could see more of this soft part of his personality. As much as I enjoyed him, being an asshole, I craved this little breakthroughs. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1381487419i/4935346._SX540_.jpg" width="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Overall, I was surprised, satisfied and had a blast while reading Fighting Destiny. I desperately needed some paranormal lovin’ and I found it in Amelia Hutchin’s book. It was raw, gritty, kinky and extremely lip biting, throw your clothes of ride I will cherish for a long, long time. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1381487419i/4935347.jpg" width="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Now, I need more Ryder and his dominant ways. My heart beats faster every time he says he want to own and ravish Syn, so I'm outta here to read next book in the series. <i> Bye ladies xx <br><br><br></i></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2583435979" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer1184610338055420513">I was a bit disappointed with this book. I don't know....I though it would be more magical, enchanting, dreamy or something like that. <br/>Maybe it is because I have read and reread so many amazing Fae books the previous week like:<br/>A Court of Thorns and Roses (A Court of Thorns and Roses, #1)<br/>A Court of Mist and Fury (A Court of Thorns and Roses, #2)<br/>Faefever (Fever, #3)<br/>Lionheart (Moonshadow, #3)<br/><br/>Naturally I thought it would be something similar and equally impressive. Unfortunately the book was more Er</span>
  <span id="freeText1184610338055420513" style="display:none">I was a bit disappointed with this book. I don't know....I though it would be more magical, enchanting, dreamy or something like that. <br />Maybe it is because I have read and reread so many amazing Fae books the previous week like:<br />A Court of Thorns and Roses (A Court of Thorns and Roses, #1)<br />A Court of Mist and Fury (A Court of Thorns and Roses, #2)<br />Faefever (Fever, #3)<br />Lionheart (Moonshadow, #3)<br /><br />Naturally I thought it would be something similar and equally impressive. Unfortunately the book was more Erotica than Fantasy which normally I wouldn't mind but this time I did mind. Maybe the timing was not correct. Not sure.<br /><br />Anyway, I still enjoyed the book and that's the reason I gave 4 stars. It certainly had an impressive start. When Synthia met the Dark Prince, aka Ryder I was ecstatic! Such a great scene! Synthia as a very powerful witch manages to bound her mortal soul to the immortal soul of the powerful fae prince. So, the prince could die if she died unless she sets him free.<br /><br />Later on she finds out that she cannot get rid off Ryder and not because she did not free his soul but because he is obsessed with her. He wants her helping him discover who kills witches and fae and for what reason. And this is the main mystery of the book. The other two mysteries are:<br /><br />1.	What exactly is Synthia? Because after a while it is obvious that she is not just a witch.<br />2.	What exactly is Ryder? Because apparently he is more than Fae.<br /><br />The backbone story is when and how Synthia and Ryder will fall in love.<br /><br />I have to say that there were parts of the book that had inconsistencies and felt like the action was stopping and then starting and then everything was flat and I was bored. <br /><br />The world building did not feel complete in many cases. The description of the vampires was non-existent and the description of Fae and Witches was lacking.<br /><br />Moreover, I don't know if it had to do with me rereading Fever series by Moning recently, but the description of “FIZ” (aka Fae Induced Zombie, aka sexually dependent slave) reminded me 100% the “priya” from the Fever series.<br /><br />The behaviour of Synthia also did not make any scene so many times. For example, why did she sign a contract with her blood without even reading it? She is a powerful witch and a very clever person, so why did she bound herself in situations and then regret it?<br /><br />On the other hand the book also had some powerful scenes like the one at the cemetery when the raised souls are dancing at the cemetery while they listen to Gun’s and Roses’ Don’t Cry and House of Pain’s Jump Around from Synthia's iPod. I loved this scene!<br /><br />Overall it is not a bad book, but it did not feel very coherent and organised. <br />Anyway, I am definitely reading the series because not all the questions have been answered :)</span>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1254709390?book_show_action=true">Apr 14, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Bookaholic (reads every mortal thing)" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Bookaholic (reads every mortal thing)" href="/user/show/25058068-bookaholic-reads-every-mortal-thing">Bookaholic (reads every mortal thing)</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="did not like it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">did not like it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/25058068-bookaholic-reads-every-mortal-thing?shelf=2015-read">2015-read</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/25058068-bookaholic-reads-every-mortal-thing?shelf=everybody-loves-but-me">everybody-loves-but-me</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/25058068-bookaholic-reads-every-mortal-thing?shelf=fantasy">fantasy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/25058068-bookaholic-reads-every-mortal-thing?shelf=paranormal">paranormal</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/25058068-bookaholic-reads-every-mortal-thing?shelf=why">why</a>,

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/25058068-bookaholic-reads-every-mortal-thing?shelf=plain-boring">plain-boring</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/25058068-bookaholic-reads-every-mortal-thing?shelf=new-adult">new-adult</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
                  <em>
                    This review has been hidden because it contains spoilers. To view it,
                    <a href="#" onclick="Effect.toggle(&#39;reviewTextContainer1254709390&#39;); return false;">click here.</a>
                  </em>
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1254709390" class="readable"
                    style="display:none"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer14618891951756586684">What? Did you expect anything different? <i>Really?</i> It's like you don't know me at all. <br/><br/>From the deplorable writing (I refuse to talk about it), to the awful Alpha-ragebeast nature of Ryder (more on that later), to the head-bangingly annoying Mary-Sueish ness of Synthia (later, later, later).<br/><br/><b>To be honest, there was <i>nothing</i> redeemable about this</b>. I can understand why many people would like this because Synthia and Ryder had some decent chemistry, but for me, all the negatives outweighed the positive</span>
  <span id="freeText14618891951756586684" style="display:none">What? Did you expect anything different? <i>Really?</i> It's like you don't know me at all. <br /><br />From the deplorable writing (I refuse to talk about it), to the awful Alpha-ragebeast nature of Ryder (more on that later), to the head-bangingly annoying Mary-Sueish ness of Synthia (later, later, later).<br /><br /><b>To be honest, there was <i>nothing</i> redeemable about this</b>. I can understand why many people would like this because Synthia and Ryder had some decent chemistry, but for me, all the negatives outweighed the positives so badly, I barely resisted the urge from flinging my kindle against the wall. The sex scenes weren't very tastefully written, and in my opinion, the 'dirty talk' made me cringe a little bit inside.<br /><br /><b>But by far, the worst feature about this book is how many spelling, grammar and punctuation mistakes were made <i>throughout</i> the book</b>. At one point, there were so many spelling errors, I almost felt like seeing how it would be on a word document (my, my, look at all those red lines).<br /><br />Synthia is an Assassin (who *snort* <b>DOESNT EVEN KILL.</b>) witch in an organisation that kills Fae. She is sent on a special suicide mission that requires her to break in a heavy security building and kidnap (or kill, I didn't get it) the Prince of Fae - only realise that it was all just a test of loyalty or some bullshit like that. Of course, at this time, our love-Interest makes a lasting first impression when <b>he starts sexually harassing information out of Synthia</b>. <br /><br />*pause* <br /><br />This would have made 0.001% of sense had it been an <i>actual mission</i> and not some twisted test, but even when Ryder was fully aware that this was just a test and not to be taken seriously, <b>he <i>still</i> tried to rape Synthia. </b>That, my friend, is not who I would call Prince Charming (or atleast, the usual Disney kind, since the Grimms Brothers are a <i>completely</i> different story when it comes to Princes).<br /><br />Moreover, the clothes Synthia wore to the mission- a black tight tank and short shorts- was not appropriate at <i>all</i>. Even I, who is about as subtle as a bull in a china shop, knows that you should wear nondescript, easy-to-shed and easy-to-move clothes while going incognito. And speaking of, I <i>get</i> that Synthia is the hottest thing since iPods and I <i>get</i> that men worship the ground she walks on, <b>but reminding me of this every page is a <i>liiitle</i> too excessive, no?</b> <br /><br />Ryder is one of the most disgusting love interest I have come across in a long time and almost physically makes me ill. He has 2 or 3 chapters in his POV, and<b> If cavemen lived today, no doubt they would sound like him</b>. Every single conversation between Synthia and him led to him repeating the word 'mine' a least a dozen times.<br /><br /><i>Synthia: I want to go.<br /><br />Ryder: No. Mine. <br /><br />Synthia: But I have a life, I have a job.<br /><br />Ryder: No you don't. Mine.<br /><br />Synthia: Boo. I'm an independent woman.<br /><br />Ryder: Mine.<br /><br />Synthia: I kill Fae-creatures like you for breakfast.<br /><br />Ryder: Mine.<br /><br />Synthia: I am a human bei-<br /><br />Ryder: Mine.<br /><br />Synthia: I have my own mi-<br /><br />Ryder: MINE! <br /><br />Synthia: *glares* Okay.</i><br /><br /><b>Aaand so it goes</b>, on and on and on. At first, the banter was tolerable, but it quickly became recycled and boring. The same arguements, the same retorts and the same recycled outcomes, <i>over and over again</i>. <br /><br />Dont believe me?<br /><br /><blockquote>
  <i> I wanted to scream, or rip his eyes out. “I’m not a piece of fucking property, I cannot be owned!” “Quite the opposite, you are mine. As of right now, you belong to me Pet"</i>
</blockquote><br /><br />Also, you would notice I left the punctuation as I read it, so there is literally <i>no comma</i> before any names or terms of (dubious) endearment in any of the dialogues. Hell, commas are almost nonexistent in the whole book and are used in completely unnecessary places. So much, that even though I'm sure the author is a really nice lady, she has <b>no clue about where to use a freaking comma</b>. <br /><br />Some of his internal monologues made me scrunch up my face so hard, my cousin brother, who was in the room with me at the time, asked me why I was (and I quote) "looking like 30 wild skunks released gas on my face" and then laughed at his own joke. He thinks he's a real comedian. But joke's on him, since he made the exact same face when I read the line aloud. <br /><br /><blockquote>
  <i>The scent of her need makes me want to pull back the delicate petals of her flower and devour it, consume it, fuck it.</i>
</blockquote> <br /><br /><b>Delicate petals of her flower, huh?</b> We both laughed so hard 10 seconds after it sunk it, I couldn't even sleep right. <br /><br />It's a really, really good thing the world in this is very similar to the one in the <i>Fever</i> series, as <b>the world building in this is piss poor</b>.Literally nothing. Nada. Even though nobody would <i>dare</i> compare this poor man's imitation of the rich, sensual world in the <i>Fever</i> series, it's certainly helpful that the concepts and world is 99% the same because then I didn't have to make up assumptions a lot. <br /><br />And before I end this (already way too long) review, I just have one thing more to ask: <br /><br /><blockquote>
  <i>"I watched you sleep,” [Ryder] replied unamused or affected by my surprise at his words that showed all over my face.</i>
</blockquote> <br /><br /><b>Edward? Is that you?</b></span>
  <a data-text-id="14618891951756586684" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

</b><br><br>I haven't slept it's early in the morning like 4 am...and <b>I am speechless and stunned</b><br><br>ha, I will post more...later...need to get a hold of myself!<br><br><b>and my thoughts, finally!</b><br><br><b>I need to clarify that I usually Do NOT read paranormal, NOT because I don't like the genre BUT because I get confused easily with the vivid description in the book when it colides with the vivid imagination in my head while trying to picture the described scene that usually involves magical stuff. And here we are coming to the point of no return cause it all depends on the author's style of writing and wheather he/she uses „heavy“ or „light“ words during the process. </b><br><br>So when I say that I was <b>mesmerised</b> with more than just the main characters' (Ryder – fae) <b>golden eyes</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1416187047ra/11908837.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I think you get my drift.<br><br><b>I was thrown into the whirpool of unimaginable world of <u>mistical creatures, fairies, faes, vampires, demons, witches, mags, warlocks and ...humans</u><br><br>but the background was set in a „normal“ human world with <u>mundane settings, like worldy music, clothes and surroundings</u>...<br><br>and when you imagine the characters powers playing out through out the book it sets another well of good vibrations and vivid displays that can only work for the one person individualy...<br><br>and the fuck it worked for me!!!</b><br><br>Adding to it the <b>scorching smut scenes</b> that really undone me, using not only magical power of the display but the words could set a trigger on me just as quickly as i was turning the pages with one touch of my finger...<br><br><b>So damn good characterisation, phenomenal badass heroine with sassy mouth and stubborness that could only lead to confortation which is phenomenaly presented through the banter of the two MCs:</b><br><br><b>Ryder</b> - the mistical fae, the Dark Prince was the sexiest and one of the most alluring male heroes my imagination could picture out...I was trembling from the first encounter with this sex on a stick and I think he will be very hard to knock down from the high place in my ranks of BBFs and sexy alphas...<br><br><b>Syn (Synthia)</b> – 21 year old witch in human form (that is actually not BUT she doesn't know it), the enforcer for the Guild that leads and protects her own coven, is one of the best female heroines I came across in a fictin world of fantasy words...<br>and <b>she's a badass, smart, powerful, bold, loyal, dedicated, sassy and passionate</b>...I loved every minute she would speak out, act out and perform...I imagine her as <b>a mix of Lara Croft and Aeon Flux, only blonde</b>...LOL<br><br><b>I liked everything about this book – the story, the surroundings, the descriptions, the dialogues, the interaction...every fuckin thing and I can honestly and without a doubt say that this was one of the best books I have read not only this year but EVER!!!<br><br>What can I say, maybe the stars were aligned in the right path for me, and this book just came into my path and knocked me on my knees...</b><br><br>So, fuck yeah, I am pleased and in need for more...<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1436199581ra/15430746.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br></span>

<div id="review_830286502" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/830286502" />
    <a title="Duchess Nicole" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/2204947-duchess-nicole"><img alt="Duchess Nicole" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1499265843p2/2204947.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/830286502?book_show_action=true">Jan 21, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Duchess Nicole" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Duchess Nicole" href="/user/show/2204947-duchess-nicole">Duchess Nicole</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2204947-duchess-nicole?shelf=dirty-talk">dirty-talk</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2204947-duchess-nicole?shelf=read-in-2014">read-in-2014</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2204947-duchess-nicole?shelf=genre-paranormal-other">genre-paranormal-other</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2204947-duchess-nicole?shelf=heroine-tstl">heroine-tstl</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2204947-duchess-nicole?shelf=highly-rated">highly-rated</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2204947-duchess-nicole?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2204947-duchess-nicole?shelf=love-triangles">love-triangles</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2204947-duchess-nicole?shelf=needs-more-hype">needs-more-hype</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2204947-duchess-nicole?shelf=recommendations">recommendations</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2204947-duchess-nicole?shelf=with-a-twist">with-a-twist</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer830286502" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer17243752606767516805">I loved, I loved, I loved this book! Going by how much I loved it, I want to give it five stars but <u>holy horrific grammar, batman!</u> It was honestly one of the most poorly edited books I've come across since the self publishing boom. The ratings are still outstanding, so readers must be overlooking it to a certain extent, but I imagine the over all feel from readers is;<br/><br/> "WHYYYYYYY...did you publish this without getting it edited?!?!?!?!? Why why why?!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!" <br/><br/>Every time I'd come across a</span>
  <span id="freeText17243752606767516805" style="display:none">I loved, I loved, I loved this book! Going by how much I loved it, I want to give it five stars but <u>holy horrific grammar, batman!</u> It was honestly one of the most poorly edited books I've come across since the self publishing boom. The ratings are still outstanding, so readers must be overlooking it to a certain extent, but I imagine the over all feel from readers is;<br><br> "WHYYYYYYY...did you publish this without getting it edited?!?!?!?!? Why why why?!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!" <br><br>Every time I'd come across a plural noun made possessive for some reason (happened dozens of times) or misspelled words, misused punctuation, or terrible grammar, I'd just have to cringe because I was LOVING the storyline, the characters, the plot to such an extreme that I actually felt bad for the author, wondering how slammed she would get from some reviewers. It's bad, folks!<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1407789659i/10765852.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1407789659i/10765853._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I'm only deducting one star for that glaring and ridiculously obvious oversight, because I hate to discourage readers from reading this <b>unless</b> you are a major stickler for bad grammar and/or this is not your usual genre and/or you don't love the pushy, ass hole alphas. <br><br>...because seriously, this "hero" takes the grand prize for ass hole. He also stole the show with his steaming sexuality and his larger than life persona. The heroine is strong yet sometimes stupid. I hate to compare it to the Fever series like so many others did, because let's face it...this needs a heavy copy and content editor before we venture into amaze-balls territory like KMM's Fever series. <b>However,</b> I can't deny that there is a certain tone to this story that gives me the same feelings as Fever. It's just really imaginative, what with all the fae and otherworldly creepy-crawlies and such. The love interest(s) and their chemistry is intense but a little slow moving, so lots and lots of build up. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1381190551ra/4486670.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>I'm very excited about moving on. I really think that if this could be pulled, fixed up, and republished, that it could make some hella waves. I hope that those reading my review look at my star rating and read through to the end, because I was blown away...by both the awful grammar AND the amazing story :D </span>
  <a data-text-id="17243752606767516805" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>
