        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer636290414" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer1710773575299325060"><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380368212ra/720761.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/> <br/><br/>I'm so glad i stumbled upon this little jewel.<br/>I love reading about fay's, especially when they are so deliciously bad.<br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/601424.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>So what to tell about Syn and Ryder.... They have this love(lust)/hate relationship, that kind of reminded me of the relationship of Raphael and Elena's from Angels' Blood by Nalini Singh. They should hate each other, but they just wanna boomshakalaka voom....<br/><br/>It's like...<br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380424629ra/846640.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/> <br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380424164ra/845538.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/> <br/><br/>and then...<br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380424629ra/846641.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/> <br/><br/>and then we go back to....<br/><br/> <img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380424629ra/846642.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/> <br/> <img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380424629ra/846643.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/> <br/> <img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380424629ra/846644.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/> <br/> <img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380424629ra/846645.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/> <br/> <img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380424629ra/846646.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>so do i have to tell that the chemistry was sizzling...YES I</span>
  <span id="freeText1710773575299325060" style="display:none"><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380368212ra/720761.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>I'm so glad i stumbled upon this little jewel.<br>I love reading about fay's, especially when they are so deliciously bad.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/601424.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>So what to tell about Syn and Ryder.... They have this love(lust)/hate relationship, that kind of reminded me of the relationship of Raphael and Elena's from Angels' Blood by Nalini Singh. They should hate each other, but they just wanna boomshakalaka voom....<br><br>It's like...<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380424629ra/846640.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380424164ra/845538.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>and then...<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380424629ra/846641.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>and then we go back to....<br><br> <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380424629ra/846642.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br> <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380424629ra/846643.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br> <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380424629ra/846644.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br> <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380424629ra/846645.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br> <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380424629ra/846646.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>so do i have to tell that the chemistry was sizzling...YES I DO!!!!<br>I almost forgot there is also a killer in the picture<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380424629ra/846647.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>but seriously now, it's a great story, it contains mystery, murder, passion and fantasy....<br>Happy reading!<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380424629ra/846648.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br></span>

<div id="review_832781777" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/832781777" />
    <a title="Sharon ∞❥ is an emotional book junkie ❥∞ " class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/3275325-sharon-is-an-emotional-book-junkie"><img alt="Sharon ∞❥ is an emotional book junkie ❥∞ " src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1514769932p2/3275325.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/832781777?book_show_action=true">Jan 23, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Sharon ∞❥ is an emotional book junkie ❥∞ " class="user" itemprop="url" name="Sharon ∞❥ is an emotional book junkie ❥∞ " href="/user/show/3275325-sharon-is-an-emotional-book-junkie">Sharon ∞❥ is an emotional book junkie ❥∞ </a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3275325-sharon-is-an-emotional-book-junkie?shelf=kindle-freebies-read">kindle-freebies-read</a>,

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3275325-sharon-is-an-emotional-book-junkie?shelf=read-in-2014">read-in-2014</a>
          </div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer832781777" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6334740135316653219">4.5 ★'s<br/><br/>Syn's a witch who works for The Guild in protecting humans. She has a bad history with the Fae so naturally when she's assigned to protect one of them, she isn't happy. Not only that but she's working closely with the Dark Prince who just pushes all her buttons! <br/><br/>I love books about witches and Fae and this one is no exception. AH has carved out her own little niche in this genre and it's almost like she's taken the best parts and incorporated them in her own story. <br/><br/>I <i>really</i> like Syn. She's</span>
  <span id="freeText6334740135316653219" style="display:none">4.5 ★'s<br><br>Syn's a witch who works for The Guild in protecting humans. She has a bad history with the Fae so naturally when she's assigned to protect one of them, she isn't happy. Not only that but she's working closely with the Dark Prince who just pushes all her buttons! <br><br>I love books about witches and Fae and this one is no exception. AH has carved out her own little niche in this genre and it's almost like she's taken the best parts and incorporated them in her own story. <br><br>I <i>really</i> like Syn. She's always trying to do the right thing but she's fallible. She's suffered some loses in her life so she's always trying to take care of her friends and the people she cares about. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1439787079ra/15884640.gif" width="400" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Ryder is a very interesting character. Intense, moody, sexy....and cruel at times. Oh yea, and he loves to talk dirty...often and A LOT! (The Fae in this story feed from emotions and they feed the best from the emotions during sex so go figure!) And bonus, we get a couple pages here and there from his POV...mainly about sex but I'm not complaining! ;) <br><br>So yeah, the sex....it's <i>scorching</i>! But it's the sexual tension that'll kill ya! Of course, Syn's going to fight it...like I said she hates the Fae but...there's some things happening that changes the way she thinks. <br><br>There are a lot of great secondary characters. Syn has her own coven, however it's small with only her and two others, Adam and Larissa. They are both great and some interesting things going on there. Ryder also has *many* interesting Fae around him that you slowly get to know. <br><br>There are some intense moments...not only with some changes that Syn is going through but with some new discoveries. There's also some sad things that happen unfortunately. <br><br>I really enjoyed almost everything in the book. Ryder's cruelty was a bit much for me and one of the sad things was, well, really sad. I'm sure that something will come from it but I don't know what it is...yet. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1400045280i/9627551.jpg" width="400" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>The ending leaves you hanging, not really a cliffhanger per se but it just ends in the middle of something. Thankfully, the next book is already out! <br><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1383320575i/6501678.jpg" width="400" height="030" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><b>Favorite quotes</b><br><br>♥ “Thanks for that by the way, not bad for a fucking Fairy—” I laughed—“get it? Fucking Fairy?” I snorted and closed my eyes.<br><br>“I get it,” he growled.”<br><br>♥ "You're looking at me like I'm a freaking Scooby Snack."<br><br>♥ “I can’t do this anymore Syn. Your silence is fucking killing me. I miss the fucking Fairy jokes, the light shining in your eyes when you smile. I can’t believe I am actually saying this…but I miss your sassy fucking mouth Pet.”<br><br>♥ “Love is more than just feeling something Syn, it's the connection of two souls that intertwine and cannot be without the other. It's not just saying you love someone, it’s showing them with every fucking breath you take, every look. It just is, simple as that. That kind of love doesn't die. It withers the soul without the other to keep it alive.”<br></span>

<br>Genre wise I would class this as urban fantasy with a big slug of paranormal romance added to the mix.<br>Syn is the heroine she’s a 21-year-old powerful witch with unknown origins and a backstory of tragedy and pain that has shaped and moulded her present self.<br>She’s a sassy takes no prisoners type with far to much attitude and pride for her own good.<br>Then we have Ryder he’s powerful fae royalty he’s also Syn’s new employer and keeper.<br>He’s as dominant as he’s delicious.<br>With a raw superiority complex and an appetite for anything sinful, he drips carnality from his very pores.<br>It’s also the essence he feeds on and he’s definitely got Syn set is his sights for an all you can eat buffet.<br>So there's a lot going on here and everything seems to track back to Syn herself.<br>Whatever is happening she’s somehow at the epicentre and both Syn and Ryder are determined to unravel the mystery of her obscure origins.<br>This one is slow-burn but still, with such amazing chemistry, it actually sizzles off the page with its raw intensity building the anticipation so expertly.<br>This is told mostly from Syn’s POV though we do get occasional obscure tidbits from Ryder as well.<br>This was an emotional rollercoaster with so many bumps along the way that you just had to hold on and hang tight for the ride.<br>It was also incredibly emotional and intense<br>This first book managed to construct the foundation and world setting things up brilliantly for the next instalment in the series and that finale definitely left me wanting more.<br><br><img <div id="review_1146212617" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1146212617" />
    <a title="Spuffed" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/14556348-spuffed"><img alt="Spuffed" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1374951642p2/14556348.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1146212617?book_show_action=true">Dec 29, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Spuffed" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Spuffed" href="/user/show/14556348-spuffed">Spuffed</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="did not like it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">did not like it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>


          <div><span class="uitext greyText">Recommends it for: </span>
           <span class="uitext reviewText">If you like mom and dad mixed in with your sexy</span></div>

        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14556348-spuffed?shelf=kinda-lame">kinda-lame</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14556348-spuffed?shelf=contrived">contrived</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14556348-spuffed?shelf=eye-roll">eye-roll</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14556348-spuffed?shelf=paranormal-scifi-fantasy">paranormal-scifi-fantasy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14556348-spuffed?shelf=predictable-made-boring">predictable-made-boring</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14556348-spuffed?shelf=did-not-finish-dumb">did-not-finish-dumb</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14556348-spuffed?shelf=action-packed">action-packed</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14556348-spuffed?shelf=author-has-no-clue">author-has-no-clue</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14556348-spuffed?shelf=hero-horrible">hero-horrible</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14556348-spuffed?shelf=heroine-horrible">heroine-horrible</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1146212617" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer2840367791967484616">Yeah, I don't want to dis an author in any review and try to avoid making it personal but really, this author just has no concept of the bigger picture. At least it seems that way to me. This book seemed to be written off an outline of bullet points and personal fantasy moments that were compiled together into a story. While I'm sure there's a plot in there somewhere (as I DNF'd it at 62%) and I wasn't terribly put off by the main dude being noting better than a rapist, I couldn't get past the c</span>
  <span id="freeText2840367791967484616" style="display:none">Yeah, I don't want to dis an author in any review and try to avoid making it personal but really, this author just has no concept of the bigger picture. At least it seems that way to me. This book seemed to be written off an outline of bullet points and personal fantasy moments that were compiled together into a story. While I'm sure there's a plot in there somewhere (as I DNF'd it at 62%) and I wasn't terribly put off by the main dude being noting better than a rapist, I couldn't get past the cluelessness of the author...<br /><br />1. Urban Fantasy This is Not: Urban Fantasies are supposed to be urban and cool. The constant name dropping of lame bands (Creed, really???), outdated slutty attire and "maybe really cool in the 90's" cars was just more than I could take. I'm fucking 37 years old and even I know this shit ain't cool. Do I have to mention Creed again? *shakes head* This is more Lame Fantasy. Fiction Writing 101: If you aren't hip to Popular Culture than do not include Popular Culture and let the reader insert their own.<br /><br />2. Lot's of Skeeved-Out Moments: Okay, so I didn't make it to the alleged rape scene at the Hunt like others did but that's because I got skeeved out more quickly than others. I wasn't cool with the way Dude was treating Chick by forcing her into sexual situations against her wishes but I went with it as I figured there was a good reason for it. But I couldn't get past the scene where the author set up a "dance leading to sexual tension" moment where the two characters are feeling their sexual appetites together while she's standing on his feet while he's dancing and she's reminded about how she did this with her father before he was murdered and then all of a sudden she's still feeling all these sexual feelings. Uh, gross. Why did you have to bring the father into sexy time? The author also did this a couple times before when Fae Dude is mind-seducing her into sex and she thinks of the tragic end of her mother who was similarly forced into sex by other Fae dudes in front of her and her father when she was only 5. Really? Dude, I do not want to think about my parents when having sex. That's not sexy, it's disturbing unless you have fantasies that lean that way. Sexy Scene Writing 101: do not include thy mother or father!!!!<br /> I've read tons of non-con and found them to be really hot in a porn like way but this was just gross and icky. I'm all for Stockholm syndrome when done right but this was all kinds of wrong.<br /><br />3. Mixed Bag of Regurgitation: Excessive Lip Biting to show vulnerability (from Twilight). "He smelled like Ambrosia" (from every 80's historical bodice ripper romance)- do you even know what ambrosia is? it's citrus fruit and sour cream *gags in mouth* and while tasty in the 19th century, I'm sure, it's a really gross thing to smell like. Snarky Sarcastic Chick (from every Chick lit book in the 2000's)- big fail as every comeback and sarcastic comment was so unfunny as to be lame and if she had said them to me, I would have literally walked away from her with a weird look on my face but without any comment because what would be the point!?! Classical Dance Lessons Scene to the song of "I've Had the Time of My Life"....uh...wha???? Waltzing to the Dirty Dancing Soundtrack? Huh? CORRECTION: apparently they are waltzing to a David Cook song which also leads to only another "huh?" from me and reinforces point #1 as being lame. Sex Scene To The Tune of "Closer" by Nine Inch Nails. Yes, Trent Resnor will always be cool but people have been having sex to this song 20+ years ago including myself. Ya got nothing new or different for us here?<br /><br />4. Three of the main male characters all had similar names. Aiden, Alden and Adam. Real big imagination, <i>Amelia.</i><br /><br />5. Lots of Missing Actions: I see this a lot in poorly written books but this one may take the cake. This is where someone is sitting then all of a sudden it turns out they are standing. Two people are in the room and then all of a sudden a Fourth person is there talking and I say "fourth" because it turns out there was a third person there too all of a sudden. It can be looked over if it happens just a few times in a book but this happened several times per chapter and it just made it so hard to read.<br /><br />6. Who, What, Huh???-- So this is a paranormal type story and yet, the author wasn't clear on all the different kinds of paranormal. There were Fae which included all kinds of different types and then there were vampires which seemed like they were a subset of Fae at one point and then they were their own class of paranormal and then they weren't???? There were witches. There were ghosts. There were different kinds of witches. There were different kind of ghosts- some who could do nothing but jump and some who could work an iPod. There were Unseelie which were the darkest Fae. And later they are the most powerful Fae and then later still, the darkest Fae but what's an unseelie? Dark, how? Most powerful, how? The Unseelie King has been hiding and or missing? Is he just King of the Unseelie or is his King of all Fae? I thought Dude was King of all Fae? But Fae are Unseelie or is it Unseelie are Fae? I don't get it. Was I supposed to study the paranormal classifications before reading this? Huh. I believe the big reveal was that Dude was the Unseelie King who was supposed to be hidden but was actually in plain sight but I'll never know cause I am not reading any more of this poo.<br /><br />7. Purely Author's Wish Fulfillment: Multiple Seduction Scenes (back to back, BTW) Via Dance Lessons all in which the Dude never really lets the Chick dance but hauls her leg around his back or something. Clearly a particular fantasy of the author. Also, note #4-- fascination with "A" names along with her own pen name. And not to forget #2-- daddy/mommy issues when it comes to sex.<br /><br />With all that being said, I was interested in what was going to happen but was continually kept eye rolling and/or grossed out most of the time that I had to stop wasting my time with this heap of shit. There is potential in the story if it could be written well and this one wasn't.</span>
  <a data-text-id="2840367791967484616" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  <span id="freeText7285939856629878687" style="display:none">DNF @ 22% with no star rating.<br /><br />Dammit!<br /><br />I love the Fae and I think had I not read the Fever series by Karen Marie Moning, I probably would have continued with this. Liked it even. But I didn't. Seriously, the Fever series is BENCHMARK. Stories should start out subtlety and not cram so much within a few pages. I need my leading men to show sweetness with their arrogance. But like I said, Ryder could have possibly changed for the better, or maybe that's how it is in his world...I'll never know.</span>

I found myself compelled by the plot and drawn in by the slow burn spicy scenes. I kept flying through pages because I was excited</span>
  <span id="freeText14907427246341501525" style="display:none">Imma be real with you: If you’re looking for a book that’s well written, well edited, and/or filled with healthy relationships, then this book is <b>NOT</b> the book for you. 🚨‼️❌🆘🚨<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1591746641ra/29621256.gif" width="498" height="278" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br>Absolutely not. Avoid forever.<br><br>So why in the hell did I, an intellectual (lol no, but humor me) feminist, enjoy this book so much?<br><br>I DON’T FUCKING KNOW OKAY. It was awesome. I couldn’t put it down. I found myself compelled by the plot and drawn in by the slow burn spicy scenes. I kept flying through pages because I was excited to see what happens next.<br><br>It kind of felt like watching Gossip Girl because...<br><br><b>1. The writing is bad.</b><br>It can be really unclear at times. For example, there is a scene where there’s an explosion. However, I didn’t even realize the explosion happened until several paragraphs later when there was a line of dialogue that literally used the word “explosion” (which I’ve now typed so many times that it now sounds weird). But then there would be other times where the writing would repeat the same sentence, but put in different words. It was like the writing was trying to summarize itself. I don’t know.<br><br><b>2. The pacing is bad.</b><br>This is mainly toward the end. Everything became super rushed. There were new conflicts, new reveals, new villains, and it all happens within the last 10% of the book. Talk about whiplash. But, I just went with it.<br><br><b>3. The character development is bad.</b><br>Couldn’t tell you the names of most of them. Everyone outside of the main two MCs are pretty generic. <br><br><b>4. The relationships are bad. </b><br>SO toxic. SO manipulative. SO anti-feminist. SO why-the-fuck-are-you-still-reading-this-Lindsey-you-hate-this-type-of-thing.<br><br><b>5. The editing is bad. </b><br>I’m aware this book is self-published, but a middle schooler could have fixed a lot of the spelling, grammatical, and syntax errors.<br><br><br>The book is a train wreck and I COULD NOT LOOK AWAY. I will probably end up reading the entire series (JUST LIKE I REWATCH GARBAGE GOSSIP GIRL EVERY YEAR.)<br><br>And...I’m not even mad about it. I enjoyed it. Idgaf. Tell a story with ridiculous drama/spice and I'm in. 😈<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1591746641ra/29621257.gif" width="500" height="280" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></span>
  <a data-text-id="14907427246341501525" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_668651179" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Zakirrah BookBlogger" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Zakirrah BookBlogger" href="/user/show/15894726-zakirrah-bookblogger">Zakirrah BookBlogger</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/15894726-zakirrah-bookblogger?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>,

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer668651179" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6161748160266206659"><b>4.5 Hot, Ryder-Loving, Fast-Paced, Fantastic Stars!!</b><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380429327i/859902._SX540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><i>Have you ever heard of the old Celtic legends of the Fae - beautiful, magical, and deadly creatures that have a love of messing with humans just for kicks and giggles?</i><br/><br/>Synthia (Syn) is a witch and she hates the Fae due to witnessing her parent be being killed by them..does that make them all evil?<br/>Can she judge them based on what a couple of them did to her parents?<br/><br/><b>"It was why they were considered the most deadly of the Otherworld.They could make</b></span>
  <span id="freeText6161748160266206659" style="display:none"><b>4.5 Hot, Ryder-Loving, Fast-Paced, Fantastic Stars!!</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380429327i/859902._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><i>Have you ever heard of the old Celtic legends of the Fae - beautiful, magical, and deadly creatures that have a love of messing with humans just for kicks and giggles?</i><br><br>Synthia (Syn) is a witch and she hates the Fae due to witnessing her parent be being killed by them..does that make them all evil?<br>Can she judge them based on what a couple of them did to her parents?<br><br><b>"It was why they were considered the most deadly of the Otherworld.They could make you like it as they fucked you to death.."</b><br> <br>The book starts out where Syn meets the Prince of the Dark Fae who wants Syn to work for him, he wants her to pose as a decoy for the dark prince of the fae Ryder's fiancée because he thinks her life is under threat..<br><br>After signing a contract and handing herself over to the Dark Fae things begin to get more complicated..Witches and Faes are being slaughtered and their body parts have been removed..<br><br>What are they doing with the body parts they are collecting? <br><br>Can Syn and Ryder find the killer and stop the murders?<br> <br><b>"..I was reckless and a loose cannon.Okay that was a little harsh.I wasn't a loose cannon-I just didn't take shit from anyone"</b><br><br>Okay so when I got this book I had forgotten what it was about when I check it out on goodreads I was like..whatt? What the hell fairies and shit? Will I even enjoy this?<br><br>The answer was <b>
  <i>hell yeah</i>
</b>!<br><br> <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380429327ra/859903.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>At the starting I was thinking hmmm what am I getting myself into?<br>And then you meet Ryder..<br><br><b>"His eyes smiled mischievously as if he was commanding me to do so.Heat flowed through me, his hands offered more support as my legs trembled once more with the need to come...His soul was fucking me from the inside and it was intensely seductive and powerful"</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380429327i/859904._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>Ryder..Ryder ahh what can I say..he bloody has me hooked, hot alpha male and so damn mysterious.<br>There is something off about him he is hiding things but what are they? Oh how I would love to jump into his head and find out!<br>Is he evil or is he the good guy?<br><br>Give me the next book right now and I will tell you!<br>Urgh how I hate waiting..<br><br>I loved Syn and Ryder's love/hate relationship it was fun and hot!<br><br>I really liked Syn's character yes yes she is a badass! She is a perfect fit for Ryder, she challenges him at each turn..<br>Cant wait to find out what will happen between them in book 2!<br><br> <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380743163i/3118149._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>Why did no-one tell me it ends on a cliffhanger?!!?<br>ahhhhhhhhhhhh the ending was like fuckkkkkk wtf is going on!! :O :O <br><br><b>"Never challenge me.I promise that you will lose.Every.Fucking.Time"</b><br><br>**ARC provided by author for an honest review**<br><br>Check out my blog for more reviews!<br><a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://zakirrahsbookblog.blogspot.co.uk/">http://zakirrahsbookblog.blogspot.co.uk/</a><br><br>Facebook: <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="https://www.facebook.com/pages/Zakirr">https://www.facebook.com/pages/Zakirr</a>..</span>
  <a data-text-id="6161748160266206659" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('IS/CjCuB9Ot766KvwJCdgvAY2AB4vFFW06Yee8r+/bqRE2GM8LAef/FHPe0J/W0RE3LV857uz3AKy3YKCh+K5A==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('+Erze42ziT6Upu64DTUCpA1Vnt+qlqUnb9la9ytvM15IdlB7VoJjqh4KcfrEWPI37j+TLEzEOwG2tDKG645EAA==')})
  }
